Question: We have three blocks. Lets call them A, B and C. A medium black square is in block A. Block B is to the right of block A. It contains a small yellow circle and one big blue square. Below and to the right of the big blue square there is the small yellow circle. Finally, we have block C which is to the right of block B. It contains a small yellow square. The small yellow square is below and to the left of a big yellow square. The big yellow square is touching the right edge of this block. What is to the right of the circle? a small yellow square or a big yellow square which is touching the right edge of a block? 0: small yellow square 1: big yellow square which is touching the right edge of a block 2: both of them 3: none of them
To solve this problem, let's analyze the positions of the objects in each block step by step:

1. **Block A**: Contains a medium black square. This block is not relevant to the question since it doesn't contain any yellow squares or circles.

2. **Block B**:
- Contains a small yellow circle and a big blue square.
- The small yellow circle is below and to the right of the big blue square.
- Since Block B is to the right of Block A, the small yellow circle is positioned somewhere in Block B, but we don't have any information about anything being to the right of the circle within Block B.

3. **Block C**:
- Contains a small yellow square and a big yellow square.
- The small yellow square is below and to the left of the big yellow square.
- The big yellow square is touching the right edge of Block C.

Now, let's determine what is to the right of the small yellow circle in Block B:

- The small yellow circle is in Block B.
- Block C is to the right of Block B.
- In Block C, the big yellow square is touching the right edge of the block, meaning it is positioned on the far right side of Block C.
- The small yellow square in Block C is below and to the left of the big yellow square, meaning it is not on the far right side of Block C.

Therefore, when considering what is directly to the right of the small yellow circle in Block B, the big yellow square in Block C, which is touching the right edge of Block C, is the object that is to the right of the circle.

Question: There are two blocks, A and B. Block A is to the left of B. Block A contains three medium yellow squares. Medium yellow square number one is touching the bottom edge of this block. This shape is below the medium yellow square number two. Block B has two medium yellow squares. Below medium yellow square number two and medium yellow square number one there is a medium black square. Medium yellow square number one is below medium yellow square number two. Which object is below a medium yellow square? the shape that is touching the bottom edge of a block or medium yellow square number one? 0: the shape that is touching the bottom edge of a block 1: medium yellow square number one 2: both of them 3: none of them
To solve this problem, let's analyze the positions of the squares in each block step by step.

**Block A:**
1. Block A contains three medium yellow squares.
2. Medium yellow square number one is touching the bottom edge of Block A.
3. Below medium yellow square number three is medium yellow square number two.
4. Below medium yellow square number three is medium yellow square number one.
5. This shape (which is not explicitly defined but is mentioned to be below medium yellow square number two) is below medium yellow square number two.

From the above, we can deduce:
- Medium yellow square number one is at the bottom of Block A.
- Medium yellow square number two is above medium yellow square number one.
- Medium yellow square number three is above medium yellow square number two.
- The shape mentioned is below medium yellow square number two, but since medium yellow square number one is at the bottom, this shape is likely medium yellow square number one itself.

**Block B:**
1. Block B has two medium yellow squares.
2. Below medium yellow square number two and medium yellow square number one, there is a medium black square.
3. Medium yellow square number one is below medium yellow square number two.

From the above, we can deduce:
- Medium yellow square number two is at the top.
- Medium yellow square number one is below medium yellow square number two.
- A medium black square is below both medium yellow square number one and medium yellow square number two.

Now, let's answer the question: Which object is below a medium yellow square? The options are:
- 0: the shape that is touching the bottom edge of a block
- 1: medium yellow square number one
- 2: both of them
- 3: none of them

In Block A:
- The shape that is touching the bottom edge of Block A is medium yellow square number one.
- There is no other object below medium yellow square number one in Block A.

In Block B:
- The medium black square is below medium yellow square number one.

Therefore, the object that is below a medium yellow square is the medium black square in Block B, which is below medium yellow square number one.

Thus, the correct answer is option 1: medium yellow square number one.

From this analysis, the only object that is below a medium yellow square is the medium black square in Block A.

1. **Block A**: Contains a medium yellow square.

2. **Block B**:
- Contains a small blue square and a big black triangle.
- The small blue square is far from, below, and to the left of the big black triangle.

- Contains a medium black triangle, a small black triangle, a medium black circle, and a small blue circle.
- Below the medium black triangle, there is a big black square.
- The medium black triangle is to the right of the small black triangle.
- To the right of and near to the medium black circle, there is the small black triangle.
- To the right of the black shape which is to the right of the medium black circle, there is the big black square.

Now, let's focus on the specific question: What is to the right of the medium black circle?

- The text states that to the right of and near to the medium black circle, there is the small black triangle.
- It also states that to the right of the black shape (which is the small black triangle) that is to the right of the medium black circle, there is the big black square.

From this, we can conclude:
- Directly to the right of the medium black circle is the small black triangle.
- The medium black triangle is not directly to the right of the medium black circle; it is to the right of the small black triangle.

The medium yellow square is in Block A, which is above Block C, and there is no indication that it is to the right of the medium black circle in Block C.

Therefore, the only shape directly to the right of the medium black circle is the small black triangle, and neither the medium black triangle nor the medium yellow square is directly to the right of the medium black circle.

- Contains a medium black square and a medium blue square.
- The medium black square is touching the bottom edge of block A and is below the medium blue square.

- Contains two medium yellow squares.

Question: There are three blocks, A, B and C. Block A is to the right of C. Block C is to the right of B. Block A has two medium yellow squares. There is also a medium black square in this block. Below medium yellow square number two and the medium black square there is medium yellow square number one. Below the medium black square there is medium yellow square number two. Block B has one medium blue square. And block C has a medium blue square. Which object is to the right of a medium blue square? medium yellow square number one or medium yellow square number two? 0: medium yellow square number one 1: medium yellow square number two 2: both of them 3: none of them
To solve this problem, let's break down the information given:

1. **Block Arrangement:**
- Block A is to the right of Block C.
- Block C is to the right of Block B.
- Therefore, the order from left to right is: Block B, Block C, Block A.

2. **Block A Details:**
- Block A contains two medium yellow squares and one medium black square.
- Below medium yellow square number two and the medium black square, there is medium yellow square number one.
- Below the medium black square, there is medium yellow square number two.

This implies:
- Medium yellow square number one is at the bottom.
- Medium yellow square number two is above medium yellow square number one.
- The medium black square is also above medium yellow square number one and is at the same level as medium yellow square number two.

3. **Block B Details:**
- Block B has one medium blue square.

4. **Block C Details:**
- Block C has one medium blue square.

Now, we need to determine which object is to the right of a medium blue square.

- Since Block B and Block C each have one medium blue square, and Block A is to the right of both Block B and Block C, any object in Block A is to the right of the medium blue squares in Block B and Block C.

- In Block A, the objects are medium yellow square number one, medium yellow square number two, and the medium black square.

- Since both medium yellow square number one and medium yellow square number two are in Block A, they are both to the right of the medium blue squares in Block B and Block C.

Therefore, the correct answer is that both medium yellow square number one and medium yellow square number two are to the right of a medium blue square.

What is above the shape which is touching the bottom edge of a block? a blue shape or a medium yellow square? 0: blue shape 1: medium yellow square 2: both of them 3: none of them
To solve this problem, let's analyze the given information step by step:

1. **Block A:**
- There are two medium black squares in Block A.
- Medium black square number one is touching the bottom edge of Block A.
- Medium black square number two is below a medium yellow square.
- Medium black square number one is below both medium black square number two and the medium yellow square.

From this, we can deduce the following arrangement in Block A:
- At the bottom of Block A is medium black square number one.
- Above medium black square number one is medium black square number two.
- Above medium black square number two is the medium yellow square.

2. **Block B:**
- Block B is above Block A.
- Block B contains one medium blue square and one medium yellow square.
- The medium blue square is below the medium yellow square in Block B.

From this, we can deduce the following arrangement in Block B:
- At the top of Block B is the medium yellow square.
- Below the medium yellow square is the medium blue square.

Now, let's address the question: "What is above the shape which is touching the bottom edge of a block?"

- The shape touching the bottom edge of a block is medium black square number one in Block A.
- Directly above medium black square number one is medium black square number two.
- Above medium black square number two is the medium yellow square in Block A.

Therefore, the shape directly above the shape touching the bottom edge of Block A (medium black square number one) is a medium yellow square.

Thus, the correct answer is option 1: medium yellow square.

It has a big black square and one medium blue triangle. The big black square is above a small black triangle and the medium blue triangle. The medium blue triangle is touching the right edge of this block. It is to the right of the small black triangle. What is to the right of the medium square? a big black square or a blue circle? 0: big black square 1: blue circle 2: both of them 3: none of them
To solve this problem, let's first visualize the arrangement of the shapes in both blocks A and B based on the given descriptions.

**Block A:**
1. There is a medium blue circle.
2. There is a big blue square.
3. There is a medium yellow square.
4. To the right of the big blue square is a medium black triangle.
5. To the right of the medium yellow square and the big blue square is the medium blue circle.

From the above, we can deduce the following order for Block A:
- The medium yellow square is to the leftmost.
- The big blue square is to the right of the medium yellow square.
- The medium black triangle is to the right of the big blue square.
- The medium blue circle is to the right of both the medium yellow square and the big blue square.

Thus, the order in Block A is:
Medium Yellow Square -> Big Blue Square -> Medium Black Triangle -> Medium Blue Circle

**Block B:**
1. There is a big black square.
2. There is a medium blue triangle.
3. The big black square is above a small black triangle and the medium blue triangle.
4. The medium blue triangle is touching the right edge of this block.
5. The medium blue triangle is to the right of the small black triangle.

From the above, we can deduce the following order for Block B:
- The big black square is at the top.
- The small black triangle is below the big black square.
- The medium blue triangle is to the right of the small black triangle and touches the right edge of Block B.

Thus, the order in Block B is:
Big Black Square (top) -> Small Black Triangle (bottom left) -> Medium Blue Triangle (bottom right)

Now, let's address the question: "What is to the right of the medium square?" The medium square in Block A is the medium yellow square.

From the arrangement in Block A:
- To the right of the medium yellow square is the big blue square.

Since Block B is to the right of Block A, we need to consider the rightmost elements of Block A and the leftmost elements of Block B.

- The rightmost element in Block A is the medium blue circle.
- The leftmost element in Block B is the small black triangle (below the big black square).

Therefore, the medium yellow square in Block A is followed by the big blue square, then the medium black triangle, and finally the medium blue circle. The big black square in Block B is not directly to the right of the medium yellow square in Block A.

Thus, the answer to the question is that the blue circle is to the right of the medium yellow square.
